    display: inline;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





There is a raw pointer `distilled_page_prefs_` stored as member variable in class DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl. And the lifetime of DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl binds to a self-owned receiver [1], which means it will stay alive as long as the underlying message pipe stays connected.



<span class="line"><!---->There is a raw pointer `distilled_page_prefs_` stored as member variable in class DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl. And the lifetime of DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl binds to a self-owned receiver [1], which means it will stay alive as long as the underlying message pipe stays connected.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





`distilled_page_prefs_` comes from DomDistillerContextKeyedService (derived from KeyedSerive) and will be a dangling pointer after the Profile is gone.



<span class="line"><!---->`distilled_page_prefs_` comes from DomDistillerContextKeyedService (derived from KeyedSerive) and will be a dangling pointer after the Profile is gone.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Because DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl can continue receiving mojo calls after the Profile is freed, a UAF would occur when function like DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl::HandleStoreFontScalingPref being invoked and accessing the raw pointer again [2].



<span class="line"><!---->Because DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl can continue receiving mojo calls after the Profile is freed, a UAF would occur when function like DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl::HandleStoreFontScalingPref being invoked and accessing the raw pointer again [2].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void CreateDistillerJavaScriptService(



<span class="line"><!---->void CreateDistillerJavaScriptService(<!----></span>



<br>





    DistillerUIHandle* distiller_ui_handle,



<span class="line"><!---->    DistillerUIHandle* distiller_ui_handle,<!----></span>



<br>





    DistilledPagePrefs* distilled_page_prefs,



<span class="line"><!---->    DistilledPagePrefs* distilled_page_prefs,<!----></span>



<br>





    mojo::PendingReceiver<mojom::DistillerJavaScriptService> receiver) {



<span class="line"><!---->    mojo::PendingReceiver&lt;mojom::DistillerJavaScriptService&gt; receiver) {<!----></span>



<br>





  mojo::MakeSelfOwnedReceiver(std::make_unique<DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl>(  // ===> [1]



<span class="line"><!---->  mojo::MakeSelfOwnedReceiver(std::make_unique&lt;DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl&gt;(  // ===&gt; [1]<!----></span>



<br>





                                  distiller_ui_handle, distilled_page_prefs),



<span class="line"><!---->                                  distiller_ui_handle, distilled_page_prefs),<!----></span>



<br>





                              std::move(receiver));



<span class="line"><!---->                              std::move(receiver));<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl::HandleStoreFontScalingPref(



<span class="line"><!---->void DistillerJavaScriptServiceImpl::HandleStoreFontScalingPref(<!----></span>



<br>





    float font_scale) {



<span class="line"><!---->    float font_scale) {<!----></span>



<br>





  distilled_page_prefs_->SetFontScaling(font_scale);   // ===> [2]



<span class="line"><!---->  distilled_page_prefs_-&gt;SetFontScaling(font_scale);   // ===&gt; [2]<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/dom_distiller/content/browser/distiller_javascript_service_impl.cc;l=45;drc=73a504d9c4206b06598fc62da68407a4a6b703b4"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/dom_distiller/content/browser/distiller_javascript_service_impl.cc;l=45;drc=73a504d9c4206b06598fc62da68407a4a6b703b4<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/dom_distiller/content/browser/distiller_javascript_service_impl.cc;l=38;drc=73a504d9c4206b06598fc62da68407a4a6b703b4"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/dom_distiller/content/browser/distiller_javascript_service_impl.cc;l=38;drc=73a504d9c4206b06598fc62da68407a4a6b703b4<!----></a>

VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 97.0.4692.71 (stable) + dev



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 97.0.4692.71 (stable) + dev<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. copy js mojo binding files to working dir



<span class="line"><!---->1. copy js mojo binding files to working dir<!----></span>



<br>





python3 ./copy_mojo_bindings.py /path/to/chrome/.../out/Asan/gen



<span class="line"><!---->python3 ./copy_mojo_bindings.py /path/to/chrome/.../out/Asan/gen<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





2. setup a HTTP server



<span class="line"><!---->2. setup a HTTP server<!----></span>



<br>





python3 -m http.server 8000



<span class="line"><!---->python3 -m http.server 8000<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





3. run out/asan/chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/xxx/ --enable-blink-features=MojoJS 



<span class="line"><!---->3. run out/asan/chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/xxx/ --enable-blink-features=MojoJS <!----></span>





http://localhost:8000/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000/poc.html"><!---->http://localhost:8000/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





4. close the tab immediately and the browser should crash in a few seconds



<span class="line"><!---->4. close the tab immediately and the browser should crash in a few seconds<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Type of crash: browser



<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash: browser<!----></span>



<br>





Crash State: see asan.log for details



<span class="line"><!---->Crash State: see asan.log for details<!----></span>

This patch moves away from using raw pointers in the distiller

<br>





javascript service, instead using a weak pointer to the main distiller



<span class="line"><!---->javascript service, instead using a weak pointer to the main distiller<!----></span>



<br>





service. Methods that call into the distiller service now check the



<span class="line"><!---->service. Methods that call into the distiller service now check the<!----></span>



<br>





weak pointer to make sure it is still alive, removing the potential



<span class="line"><!---->weak pointer to make sure it is still alive, removing the potential<!----></span>



<br>





for a use-after-free bug.



<span class="line"><!---->for a use-after-free bug.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward.
